if COREGUI:FindFirstChild(SC_UI_Name) then
    COREGUI:FindFirstChild(SC_UI_Name):Destroy()
end

ScreenGui.Parent = COREGUI
ScreenGui.ZIndexBehavior = Enum.ZIndexBehavior.Sibling
--//////////////////////////
function GetaFuncs:GetTween(object,time,easingstyle,easingdirection,properties)
    return TweenService:Create(object,TweenInfo.new(time, easingstyle, easingdirection),properties)
end
function GetaFuncs:RemoveTableDupes(tab)
	local hash = {}
	local res = {}
	for _,v in ipairs(tab) do
		if (not hash[v]) then
			res[#res+1] = v
			hash[v] = true
		end
	end
	return res  
end
function GetaFuncs:GetGameName()
    local success, info = pcall(MarketplaceService.GetProductInfo, MarketplaceService, game.PlaceId)
    if success then
        return tostring(info.Name)
    end
end
function GetaFuncs:create_commas(amount)
    local formatted = amount
    while true do  
      formatted, k = string.gsub(formatted, "^(-?%d+)(%d%d%d)", '%1,%2')
      if (k==0) then
        break
      end
    end
    return formatted
end
function GetaFuncs:MakeDraggable(topbarobject, object)
	local Dragging = nil
	local DragInput = nil
	local DragStart = nil
	local StartPosition = nil
	local function Update(input)
		local Delta = input.Position - DragStart
		local pos = UDim2.new(
				StartPosition.X.Scale,
				StartPosition.X.Offset + Delta.X,
				StartPosition.Y.Scale,
				StartPosition.Y.Offset + Delta.Y
            )
		object.Position = pos
	end
	topbarobject.InputBegan:Connect(function(input)
		if input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1 or input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch then
			Dragging = true
			DragStart = input.Position
			StartPosition = object.Position
            input.Changed:Connect(function()
                if input.UserInputState == Enum.UserInputState.End then
                    Dragging = false
                end
            end)
        end
    end)
	topbarobject.InputChanged:Connect(function(input)
        if input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseMovement or input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch then
            DragInput = input
        end
    end)
	UserInputService.InputChanged:Connect(function(input)
        if input == DragInput and Dragging then
            Update(input)
        end
    end)
end

    function SettingManager:SetTheme(Theme)
        if Theme then
            UIThemeCustom.ImageTransparency = 0
            UIThemeCustom.Image = Theme
        end
    end
    function SettingManager:SetDiscordIcon()
        local File = self.CurrentFolder.."/Cache".."/Discord.png"
        if not isfile(File) then
            local GetUrl = game:HttpGet("https://raw.githubusercontent.com/vinhuchi/rblx/main/W-azure/asset/DiscordIcon.png")
            writefile(File, GetUrl)
            repeat wait()
            until isfile(File)
        end
        UserIcon.Image = getasset(File)
    end
    function SettingManager:SetAvatar(Avatar,Id)
        
        local a,b = pcall(function()
            local Id = tostring(Id)
            local File = self.CurrentFolder.."/Cache".."/Avt.png"
            if not isfile(File) then
                local response = req(
                    {
                        Url = "https://cdn.discordapp.com/avatars/"..Id.."/"..Avatar..".png",  -- This website helps debug HTTP requests
                        Method = "GET",
                        Headers = {
                            ["Content-Type"] = "application/json"  -- When sending JSON, set this!
                        },
                    }
                )
                writefile(File,response.Body)
                repeat wait()
                until isfile(File)
            end
            UserIcon.Image = getasset(File)
        end)
        if b then
            SettingManager:SetDiscordIcon()
        end
    end
    function SettingManager:SetFolder(Folder)
        if not isfolder(Folder) then
            makefolder(Folder)
        end
        
        self.CurrentFolder = Folder
        self.Theme = self.CurrentFolder.."/Theme"
        self.Cache = self.CurrentFolder.."/Cache"
        self.AutoSave = self.CurrentFolder.."/AutoSave"
        self.AutoLoad = self.AutoSave.."/"..game.Players.LocalPlayer.Name..".txt"
        if not isfolder(self.Theme) then
            makefolder(self.Theme)
        end
        if not isfolder(self.Cache) then
            makefolder(self.Cache)
        end       
        if not isfolder(self.AutoSave) then
            makefolder(self.AutoSave)
        end           

    end
    function SettingManager:LoadAutoConfig()
        
        if not isfile(self.AutoLoad) then
            writefile(self.AutoLoad,"")
        else
            local Config = readfile(self.AutoLoad)
            if isfile(self.AutoSave.."/"..Config) then
                return HTTPS:JSONDecode(readfile(self.AutoSave.."/"..Config))
            end
        end
    end
    function SettingManager:SetAutoConfig(FileName)
        writefile(self.AutoLoad,FileName)
    end
    function SettingManager:New(FileName)
        writefile(self.AutoSave.."/"..FileName,HTTPS:JSONEncode({}))
    end
    function SettingManager:Save(FileName,Data)
        writefile(self.AutoSave.."/"..FileName,HTTPS:JSONEncode(Data))
    end
    function SettingManager:Load(FileName,Data)
        if isfile(self.AutoSave.."/"..FileName) then
            return HTTPS:JSONDecode(readfile(self.AutoSave.."/"..FileName))
        end
    end
    function SettingManager:ListFile(Mode)
        local Files = {
            ["Theme"] = "/Theme",
            ["Config"] = "/AutoSave",
        }
        --print(listfiles(self.CurrentFolder.."/Theme"))
        
        return listfiles(self.CurrentFolder..Files[Mode])
    end

                ScreenGui.Enabled = uitoggled
            end
        end
    end)

        Button_Close.ImageRectOffset = Vector2.new(924, 724)
        Button_Close.ImageRectSize = Vector2.new(36, 36)
        wait()
        local kkacc = TweenService:Create(Frame2,TweenInfo.new(.5, Enum.EasingStyle.Quart, Enum.EasingDirection.Out),{Position = UDim2.new(0,0,0,0)})
        kkacc:Play()
        kkacc.Completed:Connect(function()
            local kzkzkx = TweenService:Create(FrameCD,TweenInfo.new(getipsec, Enum.EasingStyle.Linear, Enum.EasingDirection.Out),{Size = UDim2.new(0,0,1,0)})
            kzkzkx:Play()
            kzkzkx.Completed:Connect(function()
                wait(.1)
                local kkaao = TweenService:Create(Frame2,TweenInfo.new(.5, Enum.EasingStyle.Quart, Enum.EasingDirection.Out),{Position = UDim2.new(5, 0, 1, 0)})
                kkaao:Play()
                kkaao.Completed:Connect(function()
                    wait(.2)
                    Frame:Destroy()
                end)
            end)
        end)
        Button_Close.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
            local kkaao = TweenService:Create(Frame2,TweenInfo.new(.5, Enum.EasingStyle.Quart, Enum.EasingDirection.Out),{Position = UDim2.new(5,0,0,0)})
            kkaao:Play()
            kkaao.Completed:Connect(function()
                wait(.2)
                Frame:Destroy()
            end)
        end)
    end
    function Tabs:CreateHUD(text,sec,color,rainbowntext)
        if Store1:FindFirstChild(tostring(text)) then Store1:FindFirstChild(tostring(text)):Destroy() end
        local Frame = Instance.new('Frame')
        local Frame2 = Instance.new('Frame')
        local TextLabel = Instance.new('TextLabel')
        local TextRB = rainbowntext
    
        Frame.Name = tostring(text)
        Frame.Parent = Store1
        Frame.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 22)
        Frame.BackgroundTransparency = 1

        TextLabel.Parent = Frame
        TextLabel.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(1, 1, 1)
        TextLabel.BackgroundTransparency = 1
        TextLabel.Size = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, 22)
        TextLabel.Font = Enum.Font.SciFi
        TextLabel.BorderSizePixel = 0
        TextLabel.Position = UDim2.new(2,0,0,0)
        TextLabel.Text = text
        TextLabel.AutomaticSize = Enum.AutomaticSize.X
        TextLabel.TextSize = 22
        TextLabel.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Right
        wait()
        Frame.Size = UDim2.new(0,TextLabel.AbsoluteSize.X,0,TextLabel.AbsoluteSize.Y)

        Frame2.Parent = TextLabel
        Frame2.Size = UDim2.new(0, 2, 1, 0)
        Frame2.BackgroundTransparency = 1
        Frame2.Position = UDim2.new(0,-10,0,0)
        Frame2.Size = UDim2.new(0,2,1,0)
        Frame2.BorderSizePixel = 0
        spawn(function()
            while wait() do
                Frame2.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromHSV(tick()%10/10,1,1)
            end
        end)
        if TextRB then
            spawn(function()
                while wait() do
                    TextLabel.TextColor3 = Color3.fromHSV(tick()%10/10,1,1)
                end
            end)
        else
            TextLabel.TextColor3 = color or Color3.fromRGB(73, 1, 255)
        end
        GetaHUD.Size = UDim2.new(0.1,0,0,Frame.AbsoluteSize.Y*(#Store1:GetChildren()-1))
        TweenService:Create(TextLabel,TweenInfo.new(.3, Enum.EasingStyle.Quart, Enum.EasingDirection.Out),{Position = UDim2.new(0,0,0,0)}):Play()
        wait(sec)
        local TextHUDFuncs = {}
        function TextHUDFuncs:EditText(text)
            TextLabel.Text = text
        end
        function TextHUDFuncs:Remove()
            local twdestroy = TweenService:Create(TextLabel,TweenInfo.new(.5, Enum.EasingStyle.Quart, Enum.EasingDirection.Out),{Position = UDim2.new(3,0,0,0)})
            twdestroy:Play()
            twdestroy.Completed:Connect(function()
                GetaHUD.Size = UDim2.new(0.1,0,0,Frame.AbsoluteSize.Y*(#Store1:GetChildren()-1))
                wait(.1)
                Frame:Destroy()
                wait()
            end)
            wait(sec)
        end
        return TextHUDFuncs
    end
    function Tabs:Tab(IP_title)
        local Tab = Instance.new("Frame")
        local TabDetector = Instance.new("TextButton")
        local TabTitle = Instance.new("TextLabel")
        local Frame = Instance.new("Frame")
        local UICorner = Instance.new("UICorner")
        local ContentScrolling = Instance.new("ScrollingFrame")
        local ContentFrame = Instance.new("Frame")
        local UIListLayout = Instance.new("UIListLayout")

        local totaltabcanvassize = 0

        Tab.Name = "Tab"
        Tab.Parent = TabContainer
        Tab.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
        Tab.BackgroundTransparency = 1.000
        Tab.Size = UDim2.new(0, 100, 0, 100)

        TabDetector.Name = 'TabDetector'
        TabDetector.Parent = Tab

        TabDetector.Text = ''
        TabDetector.TextTransparency = 1
        TabDetector.Position = UDim2.new(0,0,0,0)
        TabDetector.ZIndex = 3

        TabTitle.Name = "TabTitle"
        TabTitle.Parent = Tab

        TabTitle.BackgroundTransparency = 1.000
        TabTitle.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 1, 0)
        TabTitle.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
        TabTitle.Text = tostring(IP_title)
        TabTitle.TextSize = 20.000
        TabTitle.TextWrapped = true

        Frame.Parent = Tab
        Frame.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
        Frame.BorderSizePixel = 0
        Frame.Position = UDim2.new(0, 3, 0.1, 0) --//UDim2.new(0, 3, 0.1, 0)
        Frame.Size = UDim2.new(0, 3, 0, 0) --//UDim2.new(0, 3, 0.8, 0)

        UICorner.CornerRadius = UDim.new(1, 99)
        UICorner.Parent = Frame

        ContentScrolling.Name = "ContentScrolling"
        ContentScrolling.Parent = ContentContainer

        ContentScrolling.BorderSizePixel = 0

        ContentScrolling.CanvasSize = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, 0)
        ContentScrolling.ScrollBarThickness = 3

        ContentFrame.Name = "ContentFrame"
        ContentFrame.Parent = ContentScrolling
        ContentFrame.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
        ContentFrame.BackgroundTransparency = 1.000
        ContentFrame.Size = UDim2.new(0.980000019, 0, 1, 0)

        UIListLayout.Parent = ContentFrame
        UIListLayout.SortOrder = Enum.SortOrder.LayoutOrder

        if #ContentContainer:GetChildren() == 1 then
            ContentScrolling.Visible = true
            TabTitle.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
            Frame.Size = UDim2.new(0, 3, 0.8, 0) 
            Frame.Transparency = 0
        else
            ContentScrolling.Visible = false
            TabTitle.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(150, 150, 150)
            Frame.Size = UDim2.new(0, 3, 0, 0)
            Frame.Transparency = 1
        end
        TabDetector.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
            for k,p in pairs(ContentContainer:GetChildren()) do
                if p.Name == 'ContentScrolling' then
                    p.Visible = false
                end
                ContentScrolling.Visible = true
            end
            for i,v in pairs(TabContainer:GetChildren()) do
                if v.Name == 'Tab' then
                    GetaFuncs:GetTween(v.TabTitle,0.5,Enum.EasingStyle.Quart,Enum.EasingDirection.Out,{TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(150, 150, 150)}):Play()
                    GetaFuncs:GetTween(v.Frame,0.5,Enum.EasingStyle.Quart,Enum.EasingDirection.Out,{Size = UDim2.new(0, 3, 0, 0),Position = UDim2.new(0, 3, 0.1, 0),Transparency = 1}):Play()

                    GetaFuncs:GetTween(TabTitle,0.5,Enum.EasingStyle.Quart,Enum.EasingDirection.Out,{TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)}):Play()
                    GetaFuncs:GetTween(Frame,0.5,Enum.EasingStyle.Quart,Enum.EasingDirection.Out,{Size = UDim2.new(0, 3, 0.8, 0),Position = UDim2.new(0, 3, 0.1, 0),Transparency = 0}):Play()
                end
            end
        end)
        for i,v in pairs(TabContainer:GetChildren()) do
            if v:IsA('Frame') or v:IsA('TextLabel') then
                totaltabcanvassize = totaltabcanvassize+v.AbsoluteSize.Y+3
            end
        end
        TabContainer.CanvasSize = UDim2.new(0,0,0,totaltabcanvassize)

                    if v:IsA('Frame') or v:IsA('TextLabel') then
                        totalcanvassize = totalcanvassize+v.AbsoluteSize.Y
                    end
                end
                ContentScrolling.CanvasSize = UDim2.new(0,0,0,totalcanvassize)
            end
            function ContainerFunctions:Label(IP_text)
                local Label = Instance.new('Frame')
                local FrameLabel = Instance.new('Frame')
                local LabelText = Instance.new('TextLabel')
                local UICorner1 = Instance.new('UICorner')
                local UICorner2 = Instance.new('UICorner')

                if IP_customtheme then
                    Label.BackgroundTransparency = 1  
                    FrameLabel.BackgroundTransparency = 1   
                end

                local totalcanvassize = 0
                local savecontentmainsize

                Label.Name = "Label"
                Label.Parent = ContentStoreFunc
                Label.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(67, 67, 67)
                Label.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 25)
                
                FrameLabel.Name = "FrameLabel"
                FrameLabel.Parent = Label
                FrameLabel.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(30,30,30)
                FrameLabel.Size = UDim2.new(1, -4, 1, -4)
                FrameLabel.Position = UDim2.new(0,2,0,2)

                UICorner1.CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 4)
                UICorner1.Parent = Label

                UICorner2.CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 4)
                UICorner2.Parent = FrameLabel

                LabelText.Name = 'LabelText'
                LabelText.Parent = FrameLabel
                LabelText.Size = UDim2.new(1,-4,0,0)
                LabelText.Position = UDim2.new(0,2,0,2)
                LabelText.TextWrapped = true
                LabelText.BackgroundTransparency = 1
                LabelText.AutomaticSize = Enum.AutomaticSize.Y
                LabelText.Text = tostring(IP_text)
                LabelText.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
                LabelText.Font = Enum.Font.Gotham
                LabelText.TextSize = 17.000
                LabelText.TextTruncate = 'AtEnd'
                LabelText.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left
                wait()
                savecontentmainsize = UDim2.new(0,0,0,Label.AbsoluteSize.Y+5)
                ContentMain.Size = ContentMain.Size+savecontentmainsize
                for i,v in pairs(ContentFrame:GetChildren()) do
                    if v:IsA('Frame') or v:IsA('TextLabel') then
                        totalcanvassize = totalcanvassize+v.AbsoluteSize.Y
                    end
                end
                ContentScrolling.CanvasSize = UDim2.new(0,0,0,totalcanvassize)
                local ContentSettingFunctions = {}
                function ContentSettingFunctions:EditText(IP_text)
                    LabelText.Text = tostring(IP_text)
                    ContentMain.Size = ContentMain.Size-savecontentmainsize
                    savecontentmainsize = UDim2.new(0,0,0,Label.AbsoluteSize.Y+5)
                    ContentMain.Size = ContentMain.Size+savecontentmainsize
                    totalcanvassize = 0
                    for i,v in pairs(ContentFrame:GetChildren()) do
                        if v:IsA('Frame') or v:IsA('TextLabel') then
                            totalcanvassize = totalcanvassize+v.AbsoluteSize.Y
                        end
                    end
                    ContentScrolling.CanvasSize = UDim2.new(0,0,0,totalcanvassize)
                end
                return ContentSettingFunctions 
            end

                function ContentSettingFunctions:Slider(IP2_title,IP2_min,IP2_max,IP2_start,callback2)
                    local SettingSlider = Instance.new("Frame")
                    local SettingSliderTitle = Instance.new("TextLabel")
                    local SettingSliderDetector = Instance.new("TextButton")
                    local SettingSliderFrame = Instance.new("Frame")
                    local SettingSliderFrame2 = Instance.new("Frame")
                    local SettingSliderCircle = Instance.new("ImageButton")

                    local currentvalue = tonumber(IP2_start) or 0
                    local dragging = false
                    local totalcanvassize2 = 0

                    SettingSlider.Name = "SettingSlider"
                    SettingSlider.Parent = SettingFrameStoreFuncs
                    SettingSlider.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(30, 30, 30)
                    SettingSlider.BackgroundTransparency = 0
                    SettingSlider.BorderSizePixel = 0
                    SettingSlider.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 40)

                    SettingSliderTitle.Name = "SettingSliderTitle"
                    SettingSliderTitle.Parent = SettingSlider
                    SettingSliderTitle.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
                    SettingSliderTitle.BackgroundTransparency = 1.000
                    SettingSliderTitle.Position = UDim2.new(0.01, 0, 0.05, 0)
                    SettingSliderTitle.Size = UDim2.new(0.666894257, 10, 0.375, 0)
                    SettingSliderTitle.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
                    SettingSliderTitle.Text = tostring(IP2_title)..' / '..tostring(GetaFuncs:create_commas(currentvalue))
                    SettingSliderTitle.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
                    SettingSliderTitle.TextSize = 15.000
                    SettingSliderTitle.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left

                    SettingSliderDetector.Name = "SettingSliderDetector"
                    SettingSliderDetector.Parent = SettingSlider
                    SettingSliderDetector.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
                    SettingSliderDetector.BackgroundTransparency = 1.000
                    SettingSliderDetector.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 1, 0)
                    SettingSliderDetector.ZIndex = 3
                    SettingSliderDetector.Font = Enum.Font.SourceSans
                    SettingSliderDetector.Text = ""
                    SettingSliderDetector.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(0, 0, 0)
                    SettingSliderDetector.TextSize = 14.000
                    SettingSliderDetector.TextTransparency = 1.000

                    SettingSliderFrame.Name = "SettingSliderFrame"
                    SettingSliderFrame.Parent = SettingSlider
                    SettingSliderFrame.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(80, 80, 80)
                    SettingSliderFrame.BorderSizePixel = 0
                    SettingSliderFrame.ZIndex = 5
                    SettingSliderFrame.Position = UDim2.new(0.0199999996, 0, 0.699999988, 0)
                    SettingSliderFrame.Size = UDim2.new(0.94, 0, 0, 3)

                    SettingSliderFrame2.Name = "SettingSliderFrame2"
                    SettingSliderFrame2.Parent = SettingSliderFrame
                    SettingSliderFrame2.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(3, 158, 255)
                    SettingSliderFrame2.BorderSizePixel = 0
                    SettingSliderFrame2.Size = UDim2.new((IP2_start or 0) / (IP2_max or 100), 0, 1, 0)

                    SettingSliderCircle.Name = "SettingSliderCircle"
                    SettingSliderCircle.Parent = SettingSliderFrame
                    SettingSliderCircle.BackgroundTransparency = 1.000
                    SettingSliderCircle.Position = UDim2.new((IP2_start or 0)/(IP2_max or 100), -6, -2.83333325, 0)
                    SettingSliderCircle.Size = UDim2.new(0, 18, 0, 18)
                    SettingSliderCircle.ZIndex = 2
                    SettingSliderCircle.Image = "rbxassetid://3926305904"
                    SettingSliderCircle.ImageColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(3, 158, 255)
                    SettingSliderCircle.ImageRectOffset = Vector2.new(124, 124)
                    SettingSliderCircle.ImageRectSize = Vector2.new(36, 36)

                    SettingSliderDetector.MouseEnter:Connect(function()
                        GetaFuncs:GetTween(SettingSlider,0.3,Enum.EasingStyle.Quart,Enum.EasingDirection.Out,{BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(40,40,40)}):Play()
                    end)
                    SettingSliderDetector.MouseLeave:Connect(function()
                        GetaFuncs:GetTween(SettingSlider,0.3,Enum.EasingStyle.Quart,Enum.EasingDirection.Out,{BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(30,30,30)}):Play()
                    end)
                    --SettingFrameStoreFuncs.Size = SettingFrameStoreFuncs.Size+UDim2.new(0,0,0,SettingSlider.AbsoluteSize.Y)
                    for i,v in pairs(SettingFrameStoreFuncs:GetChildren()) do
                        if v:IsA('Frame') or v:IsA('TextLabel') then
                            totalcanvassize2 = totalcanvassize2+v.AbsoluteSize.Y+5
                        end
                    end
                    MainSettingFrame_2.CanvasSize = UDim2.new(0,0,0,totalcanvassize2)
                    local function move(input)
                        local pos = UDim2.new(math.clamp((input.Position.X - SettingSliderFrame.AbsolutePosition.X) / SettingSliderFrame.AbsoluteSize.X, 0, 1),-6,-2.83333325,0)
                        local pos1 = UDim2.new(math.clamp((input.Position.X - SettingSliderFrame.AbsolutePosition.X) / SettingSliderFrame.AbsoluteSize.X, 0, 1),0,1,0)
                        SettingSliderFrame2:TweenSize(pos1, "Out", "Sine", 0.15, true)
                        SettingSliderCircle:TweenPosition(pos, "Out", "Sine", 0.15, true)
                        currentvalue = math.floor(((pos.X.Scale * (IP2_max or 100)) / (IP2_max or 100)) * ((IP2_max or 100) - (IP2_min or 0)) + (IP2_min or 0))
                        SettingSliderTitle.Text = tostring(IP2_title)..' / '..tostring(GetaFuncs:create_commas(currentvalue))
                        pcall(callback2, currentvalue)
                    end
                    SettingSliderCircle.InputBegan:Connect(function(input)
                        if input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1 then
                            dragging = true
                        end
                    end)
                    SettingSliderCircle.InputEnded:Connect(function(input)
                        if input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1 then
                            dragging = false
                        end
                    end)
                    game:GetService("UserInputService").InputChanged:Connect(function(input)
                        if dragging and input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseMovement then
                            pcall(move,input)
                        end
                    end)
                end
                return ContentSettingFunctions
            end

                function ContentSettingFunctions:Slider(IP2_title,IP2_min,IP2_max,IP2_start,callback2)
                    local SettingSlider = Instance.new("Frame")
                    local SettingSliderTitle = Instance.new("TextLabel")
                    local SettingSliderDetector = Instance.new("TextButton")
                    local SettingSliderFrame = Instance.new("Frame")
                    local SettingSliderFrame2 = Instance.new("Frame")
                    local SettingSliderCircle = Instance.new("ImageButton")

                    local currentvalue = tonumber(IP2_start) or 0
                    local dragging = false
                    local totalcanvassize2 = 0

                    SettingSlider.Name = "SettingSlider"
                    SettingSlider.Parent = SettingFrameStoreFuncs
                    SettingSlider.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(30, 30, 30)
                    SettingSlider.BackgroundTransparency = 0
                    SettingSlider.BorderSizePixel = 0
                    SettingSlider.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 40)

                    SettingSliderTitle.Name = "SettingSliderTitle"
                    SettingSliderTitle.Parent = SettingSlider
                    SettingSliderTitle.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
                    SettingSliderTitle.BackgroundTransparency = 1.000
                    SettingSliderTitle.Position = UDim2.new(0.01, 0, 0.05, 0)
                    SettingSliderTitle.Size = UDim2.new(0.666894257, 10, 0.375, 0)
                    SettingSliderTitle.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
                    SettingSliderTitle.Text = tostring(IP2_title)..' / '..tostring(GetaFuncs:create_commas(currentvalue))
                    SettingSliderTitle.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
                    SettingSliderTitle.TextSize = 15.000
                    SettingSliderTitle.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left

                    SettingSliderDetector.Name = "SettingSliderDetector"
                    SettingSliderDetector.Parent = SettingSlider
                    SettingSliderDetector.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
                    SettingSliderDetector.BackgroundTransparency = 1.000
                    SettingSliderDetector.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 1, 0)
                    SettingSliderDetector.ZIndex = 3
                    SettingSliderDetector.Font = Enum.Font.SourceSans
                    SettingSliderDetector.Text = ""
                    SettingSliderDetector.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(0, 0, 0)
                    SettingSliderDetector.TextSize = 14.000
                    SettingSliderDetector.TextTransparency = 1.000

                    SettingSliderFrame.Name = "SettingSliderFrame"
                    SettingSliderFrame.Parent = SettingSlider
                    SettingSliderFrame.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(80, 80, 80)
                    SettingSliderFrame.BorderSizePixel = 0
                    SettingSliderFrame.ZIndex = 5
                    SettingSliderFrame.Position = UDim2.new(0.0199999996, 0, 0.699999988, 0)
                    SettingSliderFrame.Size = UDim2.new(0.94, 0, 0, 3)

                    SettingSliderFrame2.Name = "SettingSliderFrame2"
                    SettingSliderFrame2.Parent = SettingSliderFrame
                    SettingSliderFrame2.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(3, 158, 255)
                    SettingSliderFrame2.BorderSizePixel = 0
                    SettingSliderFrame2.Size = UDim2.new((IP2_start or 0) / (IP2_max or 100), 0, 1, 0)

                    SettingSliderCircle.Name = "SettingSliderCircle"
                    SettingSliderCircle.Parent = SettingSliderFrame
                    SettingSliderCircle.BackgroundTransparency = 1.000
                    SettingSliderCircle.Position = UDim2.new((IP2_start or 0)/(IP2_max or 100), -6, -2.83333325, 0)
                    SettingSliderCircle.Size = UDim2.new(0, 18, 0, 18)
                    SettingSliderCircle.ZIndex = 2
                    SettingSliderCircle.Image = "rbxassetid://3926305904"
                    SettingSliderCircle.ImageColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(3, 158, 255)
                    SettingSliderCircle.ImageRectOffset = Vector2.new(124, 124)
                    SettingSliderCircle.ImageRectSize = Vector2.new(36, 36)

                    SettingSliderDetector.MouseEnter:Connect(function()
                        GetaFuncs:GetTween(SettingSlider,0.3,Enum.EasingStyle.Quart,Enum.EasingDirection.Out,{BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(40,40,40)}):Play()
                    end)
                    SettingSliderDetector.MouseLeave:Connect(function()
                        GetaFuncs:GetTween(SettingSlider,0.3,Enum.EasingStyle.Quart,Enum.EasingDirection.Out,{BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(30,30,30)}):Play()
                    end)
                    --SettingFrameStoreFuncs.Size = SettingFrameStoreFuncs.Size+UDim2.new(0,0,0,SettingSlider.AbsoluteSize.Y)
                    for i,v in pairs(SettingFrameStoreFuncs:GetChildren()) do
                        if v:IsA('Frame') or v:IsA('TextLabel') then
                            totalcanvassize2 = totalcanvassize2+v.AbsoluteSize.Y+5
                        end
                    end
                    MainSettingFrame_2.CanvasSize = UDim2.new(0,0,0,totalcanvassize2)
                    local function move(input)
                        local pos = UDim2.new(math.clamp((input.Position.X - SettingSliderFrame.AbsolutePosition.X) / SettingSliderFrame.AbsoluteSize.X, 0, 1),-6,-2.83333325,0)
                        local pos1 = UDim2.new(math.clamp((input.Position.X - SettingSliderFrame.AbsolutePosition.X) / SettingSliderFrame.AbsoluteSize.X, 0, 1),0,1,0)
                        SettingSliderFrame2:TweenSize(pos1, "Out", "Sine", 0.15, true)
                        SettingSliderCircle:TweenPosition(pos, "Out", "Sine", 0.15, true)
                        currentvalue = math.floor(((pos.X.Scale * (IP2_max or 100)) / (IP2_max or 100)) * ((IP2_max or 100) - (IP2_min or 0)) + (IP2_min or 0))
                        SettingSliderTitle.Text = tostring(IP2_title)..' / '..tostring(GetaFuncs:create_commas(currentvalue))
                        pcall(callback2, currentvalue)
                    end
                    SettingSliderCircle.InputBegan:Connect(function(input)
                        if input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1 then
                            dragging = true
                        end
                    end)
                    SettingSliderCircle.InputEnded:Connect(function(input)
                        if input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1 then
                            dragging = false
                        end
                    end)
                    game:GetService("UserInputService").InputChanged:Connect(function(input)
                        if dragging and input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseMovement then
                            pcall(move,input)
                        end
                    end)
                end
                return ContentSettingFunctions
            end
            function ContainerFunctions:Toggle(IP_title,IP_description,IP_startbool,IP_settingtitle,callback)
                if IP_description == nil or IP_description == '' then
                    IP_description = 'Blank'
                end
                if IP_title == nil or IP_title == '' then
                      IP_title = 'Blank'
                end
                local Toggle = Instance.new("Frame")
                local UICorner = Instance.new("UICorner")
                local ToggleSettingInfo = Instance.new("Frame")
                local UICorner_2 = Instance.new("UICorner")
                local ToggleSettingInfo2 = Instance.new("Frame")
                local IconSettingInfo = Instance.new("ImageButton")
                local ToggleTitle = Instance.new("TextLabel")
                local ToggleDescription = Instance.new("TextLabel")
                local ToggleSwitch = Instance.new("Frame")
                local ToggleSwitch2 = Instance.new("Frame")
                local UICorner_3 = Instance.new("UICorner")
                local ToggleCircle = Instance.new("ImageButton")
                local UICorner_4 = Instance.new("UICorner")
                local ToggleDetector = Instance.new("TextButton")
                local ContentSetting = Instance.new("Frame")
                local BlurSetting = Instance.new("Frame")

                    wait()

                    SettingSliderCircle.Name = "SettingSliderCircle"
                    SettingSliderCircle.Parent = SettingSliderFrame
                    SettingSliderCircle.BackgroundTransparency = 1.000
                    SettingSliderCircle.Position = UDim2.new((IP2_start or 0)/(IP2_max or 100), -6, -2.83333325, 0)

                    SettingSliderCircle.ZIndex = 2
                    SettingSliderCircle.Image = "rbxassetid://3926305904"
                    SettingSliderCircle.ImageColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(3, 158, 255)

                        GetaFuncs:GetTween(SettingSlider,0.3,Enum.EasingStyle.Quart,Enum.EasingDirection.Out,{BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(40,40,40)}):Play()
                    end)
                    SettingSliderDetector.MouseLeave:Connect(function()
                        GetaFuncs:GetTween(SettingSlider,0.3,Enum.EasingStyle.Quart,Enum.EasingDirection.Out,{BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(30,30,30)}):Play()
                    end)
                    --SettingFrameStoreFuncs.Size = SettingFrameStoreFuncs.Size+UDim2.new(0,0,0,SettingSlider.AbsoluteSize.Y)
                    for i,v in pairs(SettingFrameStoreFuncs:GetChildren()) do
                        if v:IsA('Frame') or v:IsA('TextLabel') then
                            totalcanvassize2 = totalcanvassize2+v.AbsoluteSize.Y+5
                        end
                    end
                    MainSettingFrame_2.CanvasSize = UDim2.new(0,0,0,totalcanvassize2)
                    local function move(input)
                        local pos = UDim2.new(math.clamp((input.Position.X - SettingSliderFrame.AbsolutePosition.X) / SettingSliderFrame.AbsoluteSize.X, 0, 1),-6,-2.83333325,0)
                        local pos1 = UDim2.new(math.clamp((input.Position.X - SettingSliderFrame.AbsolutePosition.X) / SettingSliderFrame.AbsoluteSize.X, 0, 1),0,1,0)
                        SettingSliderFrame2:TweenSize(pos1, "Out", "Sine", 0.15, true)
                        SettingSliderCircle:TweenPosition(pos, "Out", "Sine", 0.15, true)
                        currentvalue = math.floor(((pos.X.Scale * (IP2_max or 100)) / (IP2_max or 100)) * ((IP2_max or 100) - (IP2_min or 0)) + (IP2_min or 0))
                        SettingSliderTitle.Text = tostring(IP2_title)..' / '..tostring(GetaFuncs:create_commas(currentvalue))
                        pcall(callback2, currentvalue)
                    end
                    SettingSliderCircle.InputBegan:Connect(function(input)
                        if input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1 then
                            dragging = true
                        end
                    end)
                    SettingSliderCircle.InputEnded:Connect(function(input)
                        if input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1 then
                            dragging = false
                        end
                    end)
                    game:GetService("UserInputService").InputChanged:Connect(function(input)
                        if dragging and input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseMovement then
                            pcall(move,input)
                        end
                    end)
                end
                return ContentSettingFunctions
            end

                    SettingToggleDetector.TextSize = 14.000
                    SettingToggleDetector.TextTransparency = 1.000

                    --SettingFrameStoreFuncs.Size = SettingFrameStoreFuncs.Size+UDim2.new(0,0,0,SettingSlider.AbsoluteSize.Y)
                    for i,v in pairs(SettingFrameStoreFuncs:GetChildren()) do
                        if v:IsA('Frame') or v:IsA('TextLabel') then
                            totalcanvassize2 = totalcanvassize2+v.AbsoluteSize.Y+5
                        end
                    end
                    MainSettingFrame_2.CanvasSize = UDim2.new(0,0,0,totalcanvassize2)

                    if togglebool2 then
                        GetaFuncs:GetTween(SettingToggleCircle,0.3,Enum.EasingStyle.Quart,Enum.EasingDirection.Out,{Position = UDim2.new(0.545, 0, 0, 2),ImageColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255,255,255)}):Play()
                        GetaFuncs:GetTween(SettingToggleFrame1,0.3,Enum.EasingStyle.Quart,Enum.EasingDirection.Out,{BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(0,153,255)}):Play()
                        GetaFuncs:GetTween(SettingToggleFrame2,0.3,Enum.EasingStyle.Quart,Enum.EasingDirection.Out,{BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(0,153,255)}):Play()

                        wait(0.1)
                        togglebool2 = true

                    end

                            togglebool2 = true
                            pcall(callback2,togglebool2)
                        end
                    end)
                    SettingToggleDetector.MouseEnter:Connect(function()
                        GetaFuncs:GetTween(SettingToggle,0.3,Enum.EasingStyle.Quart,Enum.EasingDirection.Out,{BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(40,40,40)}):Play()
                    end)

                        GetaFuncs:GetTween(SettingToggle,0.3,Enum.EasingStyle.Quart,Enum.EasingDirection.Out,{BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(30,30,30)}):Play()
                    end)
                end
                function ContentSettingFunctions:Slider(IP2_title,IP2_min,IP2_max,IP2_start,callback2)
                    local SettingSlider = Instance.new("Frame")
                    local SettingSliderTitle = Instance.new("TextLabel")
                    local SettingSliderDetector = Instance.new("TextButton")
                    local SettingSliderFrame = Instance.new("Frame")
                    local SettingSliderFrame2 = Instance.new("Frame")
                    local SettingSliderCircle = Instance.new("ImageButton")

                    local currentvalue = tonumber(IP2_start) or 0
                    local dragging = false
                    local totalcanvassize2 = 0

                    SettingSlider.Name = "SettingSlider"
                    SettingSlider.Parent = SettingFrameStoreFuncs
                    SettingSlider.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(30, 30, 30)
                    SettingSlider.BackgroundTransparency = 0
                    SettingSlider.BorderSizePixel = 0
                    SettingSlider.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 40)

                    SettingSliderTitle.Name = "SettingSliderTitle"
                    SettingSliderTitle.Parent = SettingSlider
                    SettingSliderTitle.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
                    SettingSliderTitle.BackgroundTransparency = 1.000
                    SettingSliderTitle.Position = UDim2.new(0.01, 0, 0.05, 0)
                    SettingSliderTitle.Size = UDim2.new(0.666894257, 10, 0.375, 0)
                    SettingSliderTitle.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
                    SettingSliderTitle.Text = tostring(IP2_title)..' / '..tostring(GetaFuncs:create_commas(currentvalue))
                    SettingSliderTitle.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
                    SettingSliderTitle.TextSize = 15.000
                    SettingSliderTitle.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left

                    SettingSliderDetector.Name = "SettingSliderDetector"
                    SettingSliderDetector.Parent = SettingSlider
                    SettingSliderDetector.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
                    SettingSliderDetector.BackgroundTransparency = 1.000
                    SettingSliderDetector.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 1, 0)
                    SettingSliderDetector.ZIndex = 3
                    SettingSliderDetector.Font = Enum.Font.SourceSans
                    SettingSliderDetector.Text = ""
                    SettingSliderDetector.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(0, 0, 0)
                    SettingSliderDetector.TextSize = 14.000
                    SettingSliderDetector.TextTransparency = 1.000

                    SettingSliderFrame.Name = "SettingSliderFrame"
                    SettingSliderFrame.Parent = SettingSlider
                    SettingSliderFrame.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(80, 80, 80)
                    SettingSliderFrame.BorderSizePixel = 0
                    SettingSliderFrame.ZIndex = 5
                    SettingSliderFrame.Position = UDim2.new(0.0199999996, 0, 0.699999988, 0)
                    SettingSliderFrame.Size = UDim2.new(0.94, 0, 0, 3)

                    SettingSliderFrame2.Name = "SettingSliderFrame2"
                    SettingSliderFrame2.Parent = SettingSliderFrame
                    SettingSliderFrame2.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(3, 158, 255)
                    SettingSliderFrame2.BorderSizePixel = 0
                    SettingSliderFrame2.Size = UDim2.new((IP2_start or 0) / (IP2_max or 100), 0, 1, 0)

                    SettingSliderCircle.Name = "SettingSliderCircle"
                    SettingSliderCircle.Parent = SettingSliderFrame
                    SettingSliderCircle.BackgroundTransparency = 1.000
                    SettingSliderCircle.Position = UDim2.new((IP2_start or 0)/(IP2_max or 100), -6, -2.83333325, 0)
                    SettingSliderCircle.Size = UDim2.new(0, 18, 0, 18)
                    SettingSliderCircle.ZIndex = 2
                    SettingSliderCircle.Image = "rbxassetid://3926305904"
                    SettingSliderCircle.ImageColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(3, 158, 255)
                    SettingSliderCircle.ImageRectOffset = Vector2.new(124, 124)
                    SettingSliderCircle.ImageRectSize = Vector2.new(36, 36)

                    SettingSliderDetector.MouseEnter:Connect(function()
                        GetaFuncs:GetTween(SettingSlider,0.3,Enum.EasingStyle.Quart,Enum.EasingDirection.Out,{BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(40,40,40)}):Play()
                    end)
                    SettingSliderDetector.MouseLeave:Connect(function()
                        GetaFuncs:GetTween(SettingSlider,0.3,Enum.EasingStyle.Quart,Enum.EasingDirection.Out,{BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(30,30,30)}):Play()
                    end)
                    --SettingFrameStoreFuncs.Size = SettingFrameStoreFuncs.Size+UDim2.new(0,0,0,SettingSlider.AbsoluteSize.Y)
                    for i,v in pairs(SettingFrameStoreFuncs:GetChildren()) do
                        if v:IsA('Frame') or v:IsA('TextLabel') then
                            totalcanvassize2 = totalcanvassize2+v.AbsoluteSize.Y+5
                        end
                    end
                    MainSettingFrame_2.CanvasSize = UDim2.new(0,0,0,totalcanvassize2)
                    local function move(input)
                        local pos = UDim2.new(math.clamp((input.Position.X - SettingSliderFrame.AbsolutePosition.X) / SettingSliderFrame.AbsoluteSize.X, 0, 1),-6,-2.83333325,0)
                        local pos1 = UDim2.new(math.clamp((input.Position.X - SettingSliderFrame.AbsolutePosition.X) / SettingSliderFrame.AbsoluteSize.X, 0, 1),0,1,0)
                        SettingSliderFrame2:TweenSize(pos1, "Out", "Sine", 0.15, true)
                        SettingSliderCircle:TweenPosition(pos, "Out", "Sine", 0.15, true)
                        currentvalue = math.floor(((pos.X.Scale * (IP2_max or 100)) / (IP2_max or 100)) * ((IP2_max or 100) - (IP2_min or 0)) + (IP2_min or 0))
                        SettingSliderTitle.Text = tostring(IP2_title)..' / '..tostring(GetaFuncs:create_commas(currentvalue))
                        pcall(callback2, currentvalue)
                    end
                    SettingSliderCircle.InputBegan:Connect(function(input)
                        if input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1 then
                            dragging = true
                        end
                    end)
                    SettingSliderCircle.InputEnded:Connect(function(input)
                        if input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1 then
                            dragging = false
                        end
                    end)
                    game:GetService("UserInputService").InputChanged:Connect(function(input)
                        if dragging and input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseMovement then
                            pcall(move,input)
                        end
                    end)
                end
                return ContentSettingFunctions
            end

                local function move(input)
                    local pos = UDim2.new(math.clamp((input.Position.X - SlideFrame.AbsolutePosition.X) / SlideFrame.AbsoluteSize.X, 0, 1),-6,-2.83333325,0)
                    local pos1 = UDim2.new(math.clamp((input.Position.X - SlideFrame.AbsolutePosition.X) / SlideFrame.AbsoluteSize.X, 0, 1),0,1,0)
                    CurrentSlide:TweenSize(pos1, "Out", "Sine", 0.15, true)
                    SlideCircle:TweenPosition(pos, "Out", "Sine", 0.15, true)
                    currentvalue = math.floor(((pos.X.Scale * (IP_max or 100)) / (IP_max or 100)) * ((IP_max or 100) - (IP_min or 0)) + (IP_min or 0))
                    SliderValue.Text = tostring(GetaFuncs:create_commas(currentvalue))
                    pcall(callback, currentvalue)
                end     
                InputSlideEdit.FocusLost:Connect(function()
                    if tonumber(InputSlideEdit.Text) then
                        local getInputSlider = math.round(tonumber(InputSlideEdit.Text))
                        if getInputSlider >= IP_min and getInputSlider >= IP_max then
                            currentvalue = IP_max
                        elseif getInputSlider >= IP_min and getInputSlider < IP_max then
                            currentvalue = getInputSlider
                        elseif getInputSlider < IP_min  then
                            currentvalue = IP_min
                        end
                        local pos = UDim2.new(currentvalue/IP_max,-6,-2.83333325,0)
                        local pos1 = UDim2.new(currentvalue/IP_max,0,1,0)
                        CurrentSlide:TweenSize(pos1, "Out", "Sine", 0.2, true)
                        SlideCircle:TweenPosition(pos, "Out", "Sine", 0.2, true)
                        SliderValue.Text = tostring(GetaFuncs:create_commas(currentvalue))
                        pcall(callback, currentvalue)
                    end
                end)
                SliderReset.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
                    local slidertw = GetaFuncs:GetTween(SliderReset,0.1,Enum.EasingStyle.Quart,Enum.EasingDirection.Out,{ImageColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255,255,255)})
                    local slidertw2 = GetaFuncs:GetTween(SliderReset,0.1,Enum.EasingStyle.Quart,Enum.EasingDirection.Out,{ImageColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(80,80,80)})
                    local slidertw3 = GetaFuncs:GetTween(SliderReset,1,Enum.EasingStyle.Sine,Enum.EasingDirection.Out,{Rotation = -360})
                    slidertw3:Play()
                    slidertw:Play()
                    local pos = UDim2.new((IP_resetvalue or IP_start)/IP_max,-6,-2.83333325,0)
                    local pos1 = UDim2.new((IP_resetvalue or IP_start)/IP_max,0,1,0)
                    CurrentSlide:TweenSize(pos1, "Out", "Sine", 0.2, true)
                    SlideCircle:TweenPosition(pos, "Out", "Sine", 0.2, true)
                    currentvalue = IP_resetvalue or IP_start
                    SliderValue.Text = tostring(GetaFuncs:create_commas(currentvalue))
                    slidertw3.Completed:Connect(function()
                        SliderReset.Rotation = 0
                    end)
                    slidertw.Completed:Connect(function()
                        slidertw2:Play()
                        pcall(callback, currentvalue)
                        wait(.1)
                    end)
                end)
                SliderIncrease.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
                    if currentvalue < IP_max then
                        local slidertw = GetaFuncs:GetTween(SliderIncrease,0.1,Enum.EasingStyle.Quart,Enum.EasingDirection.Out,{ImageColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255,255,255)})
                        local slidertw2 = GetaFuncs:GetTween(SliderIncrease,0.1,Enum.EasingStyle.Quart,Enum.EasingDirection.Out,{ImageColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(80,80,80)})
                        slidertw:Play()
                        if currentvalue+IP_increasevalue <= IP_max then
                            local pos = UDim2.new((currentvalue+IP_increasevalue)/IP_max,-6,-2.83333325,0)
                            local pos1 = UDim2.new((currentvalue+IP_increasevalue)/IP_max,0,1,0)
                            CurrentSlide:TweenSize(pos1, "Out", "Sine", 0.2, true)
                            SlideCircle:TweenPosition(pos, "Out", "Sine", 0.2, true)
                            currentvalue = (currentvalue+IP_increasevalue)
                            SliderValue.Text = tostring(GetaFuncs:create_commas(currentvalue))
                            slidertw.Completed:Connect(function()
                                slidertw2:Play()
                                pcall(callback, currentvalue)
                                wait(.1)
                            end)
                        else
                            local pos = UDim2.new(IP_max/IP_max,-6,-2.83333325,0)
                            local pos1 = UDim2.new(IP_max/IP_max,0,1,0)
                            CurrentSlide:TweenSize(pos1, "Out", "Sine", 0.2, true)
                            SlideCircle:TweenPosition(pos, "Out", "Sine", 0.2, true)
                            currentvalue = IP_max
                            SliderValue.Text = tostring(GetaFuncs:create_commas(currentvalue))
                            slidertw.Completed:Connect(function()
                                slidertw2:Play()
                                pcall(callback, currentvalue)
                                wait(.1)
                            end)
                        end
                    end
                end)
                SliderDecrease.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
                    if currentvalue > IP_min then
                        local slidertw = GetaFuncs:GetTween(SliderDecrease,0.1,Enum.EasingStyle.Quart,Enum.EasingDirection.Out,{ImageColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255,255,255)})
                        local slidertw2 = GetaFuncs:GetTween(SliderDecrease,0.1,Enum.EasingStyle.Quart,Enum.EasingDirection.Out,{ImageColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(80,80,80)})
                        slidertw:Play()
                        if currentvalue-IP_increasevalue >= IP_min then
                            local pos = UDim2.new((currentvalue-IP_decreasevalue)/IP_max,-6,-2.83333325,0)
                            local pos1 = UDim2.new((currentvalue-IP_decreasevalue)/IP_max,0,1,0)
                            CurrentSlide:TweenSize(pos1, "Out", "Sine", 0.2, true)
                            SlideCircle:TweenPosition(pos, "Out", "Sine", 0.2, true)
                            currentvalue = (currentvalue-IP_decreasevalue)
                            SliderValue.Text = tostring(GetaFuncs:create_commas(currentvalue))
                            slidertw.Completed:Connect(function()
                                slidertw2:Play()
                                pcall(callback, currentvalue)
                                wait(.1)
                            end)
                        else
                            local pos = UDim2.new(IP_min/IP_max,-6,-2.83333325,0)
                            local pos1 = UDim2.new(IP_min/IP_max,0,1,0)
                            CurrentSlide:TweenSize(pos1, "Out", "Sine", 0.2, true)
                            SlideCircle:TweenPosition(pos, "Out", "Sine", 0.2, true)
                            currentvalue = IP_min
                            SliderValue.Text = tostring(GetaFuncs:create_commas(currentvalue))
                            slidertw.Completed:Connect(function()
                                slidertw2:Play()
                                pcall(callback, currentvalue)
                                wait(.1)
                            end)
                        end
                    end
                end)
                SlideCircle.InputBegan:Connect(function(input)
                    if input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1 then
                        dragging = true
                    end
                end)
                SlideCircle.InputEnded:Connect(function(input)
                    if input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1 then
                        dragging = false
                    end
                end)
                game:GetService("UserInputService").InputChanged:Connect(function(input)
                    if dragging and input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseMovement then
                        pcall(move,input)
                    end
                end)
                SliderDetector.MouseEnter:Connect(function()
                    GetaFuncs:GetTween(Slider,0.3,Enum.EasingStyle.Quart,Enum.EasingDirection.Out,{BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(40,40,40)}):Play()
                end)

                end)

                        end
                    end
                    MainSettingFrame_2.CanvasSize = UDim2.new(0,0,0,totalcanvassize2)
                    local function move(input)
                        local pos = UDim2.new(math.clamp((input.Position.X - SettingSliderFrame.AbsolutePosition.X) / SettingSliderFrame.AbsoluteSize.X, 0, 1),-6,-2.83333325,0)
                        local pos1 = UDim2.new(math.clamp((input.Position.X - SettingSliderFrame.AbsolutePosition.X) / SettingSliderFrame.AbsoluteSize.X, 0, 1),0,1,0)
                        SettingSliderFrame2:TweenSize(pos1, "Out", "Sine", 0.15, true)
                        SettingSliderCircle:TweenPosition(pos, "Out", "Sine", 0.15, true)
                        currentvalue = math.floor(((pos.X.Scale * (IP2_max or 100)) / (IP2_max or 100)) * ((IP2_max or 100) - (IP2_min or 0)) + (IP2_min or 0))
                        SettingSliderTitle.Text = tostring(IP2_title)..' / '..tostring(GetaFuncs:create_commas(currentvalue))
                        pcall(callback2, currentvalue)
                    end
                    SettingSliderCircle.InputBegan:Connect(function(input)
                        if input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1 then
                            dragging = true
                        end
                    end)
                    SettingSliderCircle.InputEnded:Connect(function(input)
                        if input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1 then
                            dragging = false
                        end
                    end)
                    game:GetService("UserInputService").InputChanged:Connect(function(input)
                        if dragging and input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseMovement then
                            pcall(move,input)
                        end
                    end)
                end
                return ContentSettingFunctions
            end

                local ContentSettingFunctions = {}
                function ContentSettingFunctions:CreateItem(IP2_title)

                    local ItemFrame = Instance.new("Frame")
                    local UICorner = Instance.new("UICorner")
                    local ItemFrame2 = Instance.new("Frame")

                        DropdownValue.Text = ItemName.Text
                        dropdowntoggled = false
                        local dwtw1 = GetaFuncs:GetTween(DropdownContainerFrame,0.3,Enum.EasingStyle.Quart,Enum.EasingDirection.Out,{Size = UDim2.new(1,0,0,0)})
                        GetaFuncs:GetTween(DropdownShow,0.3,Enum.EasingStyle.Quart,Enum.EasingDirection.Out,{ImageColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(147, 147, 147),Rotation = 180}):Play()
                        GetaFuncs:GetTween(Dropdown,0.3,Enum.EasingStyle.Quart,Enum.EasingDirection.Out,{Size = UDim2.new(1,0,0,70)}):Play()
                        dwtw1:Play()
                        dwtw1.Completed:Connect(function()
                            DropdownContainerFrame.Visible = false
                        end)
                        pcall(callback,ItemName.Text)
                    end)
                end
                function ContentSettingFunctions:UpdateTitle(IP2_title)
                    DropdownTitle.Text = IP2_title
                end
                function ContentSettingFunctions:UpdateDescription(IP2_desc)
                    DropdownDescription.Text = IP2_desc
                end
                function ContentSettingFunctions:ClearItems()
                    for i,v in pairs(DropdownContainer:GetChildren()) do
                        if v:IsA('Frame') then
                            v:Destroy()
                        end
                    end
                    DropdownContainer.CanvasSize = UDim2.new(0,0,0,0)
                end
                function ContentSettingFunctions:UpdateItems(IP2_list)
                    --DropdownFunctions:Clear()
                    wait()
                    ContentSettingFunctions:ClearItems()
                    for i,v in pairs(IP2_list) do
                        ContentSettingFunctions:CreateItem(tostring(v))
                    end
                end
                function ContentSettingFunctions:AddItem(IP2_name)
                    ContentSettingFunctions:CreateItem(tostring(IP2_name))
                end
                function ContentSettingFunctions:RemoveItem(IP2_name)
                    for i,v in pairs(DropdownContainer:GetChildren()) do
                        if v.Name == IP2_name then
                            v:Destroy()
                            DropdownContainer.CanvasSize = DropdownContainer.CanvasSize-UDim2.new(0,0,0,33)
                        end
                    end
                end
                ContentSettingFunctions:UpdateItems(IP_list)

                function ContentSettingFunctions:Slider(IP2_title,IP2_min,IP2_max,IP2_start,callback2)
                    local SettingSlider = Instance.new("Frame")
                    local SettingSliderTitle = Instance.new("TextLabel")
                    local SettingSliderDetector = Instance.new("TextButton")
                    local SettingSliderFrame = Instance.new("Frame")
                    local SettingSliderFrame2 = Instance.new("Frame")
                    local SettingSliderCircle = Instance.new("ImageButton")

                    local currentvalue = tonumber(IP2_start) or 0
                    local dragging = false
                    local totalcanvassize2 = 0

                    SettingSlider.Name = "SettingSlider"
                    SettingSlider.Parent = SettingFrameStoreFuncs
                    SettingSlider.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(30, 30, 30)
                    SettingSlider.BackgroundTransparency = 0
                    SettingSlider.BorderSizePixel = 0
                    SettingSlider.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 40)

                    SettingSliderTitle.Name = "SettingSliderTitle"
                    SettingSliderTitle.Parent = SettingSlider
                    SettingSliderTitle.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
                    SettingSliderTitle.BackgroundTransparency = 1.000
                    SettingSliderTitle.Position = UDim2.new(0.01, 0, 0.05, 0)
                    SettingSliderTitle.Size = UDim2.new(0.666894257, 10, 0.375, 0)
                    SettingSliderTitle.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
                    SettingSliderTitle.Text = tostring(IP2_title)..' / '..tostring(GetaFuncs:create_commas(currentvalue))
                    SettingSliderTitle.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
                    SettingSliderTitle.TextSize = 15.000
                    SettingSliderTitle.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left

                    SettingSliderDetector.Name = "SettingSliderDetector"
                    SettingSliderDetector.Parent = SettingSlider
                    SettingSliderDetector.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
                    SettingSliderDetector.BackgroundTransparency = 1.000
                    SettingSliderDetector.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 1, 0)
                    SettingSliderDetector.ZIndex = 3
                    SettingSliderDetector.Font = Enum.Font.SourceSans
                    SettingSliderDetector.Text = ""
                    SettingSliderDetector.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(0, 0, 0)
                    SettingSliderDetector.TextSize = 14.000
                    SettingSliderDetector.TextTransparency = 1.000

                    SettingSliderFrame.Name = "SettingSliderFrame"
                    SettingSliderFrame.Parent = SettingSlider
                    SettingSliderFrame.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(80, 80, 80)
                    SettingSliderFrame.BorderSizePixel = 0
                    SettingSliderFrame.ZIndex = 5
                    SettingSliderFrame.Position = UDim2.new(0.0199999996, 0, 0.699999988, 0)
                    SettingSliderFrame.Size = UDim2.new(0.94, 0, 0, 3)

                    SettingSliderFrame2.Name = "SettingSliderFrame2"
                    SettingSliderFrame2.Parent = SettingSliderFrame
                    SettingSliderFrame2.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(3, 158, 255)
                    SettingSliderFrame2.BorderSizePixel = 0
                    SettingSliderFrame2.Size = UDim2.new((IP2_start or 0) / (IP2_max or 100), 0, 1, 0)

                    SettingSliderCircle.Name = "SettingSliderCircle"
                    SettingSliderCircle.Parent = SettingSliderFrame
                    SettingSliderCircle.BackgroundTransparency = 1.000
                    SettingSliderCircle.Position = UDim2.new((IP2_start or 0)/(IP2_max or 100), -6, -2.83333325, 0)
                    SettingSliderCircle.Size = UDim2.new(0, 18, 0, 18)
                    SettingSliderCircle.ZIndex = 2
                    SettingSliderCircle.Image = "rbxassetid://3926305904"
                    SettingSliderCircle.ImageColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(3, 158, 255)
                    SettingSliderCircle.ImageRectOffset = Vector2.new(124, 124)
                    SettingSliderCircle.ImageRectSize = Vector2.new(36, 36)

                    SettingSliderDetector.MouseEnter:Connect(function()
                        GetaFuncs:GetTween(SettingSlider,0.3,Enum.EasingStyle.Quart,Enum.EasingDirection.Out,{BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(40,40,40)}):Play()
                    end)
                    SettingSliderDetector.MouseLeave:Connect(function()
                        GetaFuncs:GetTween(SettingSlider,0.3,Enum.EasingStyle.Quart,Enum.EasingDirection.Out,{BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(30,30,30)}):Play()
                    end)
                    --SettingFrameStoreFuncs.Size = SettingFrameStoreFuncs.Size+UDim2.new(0,0,0,SettingSlider.AbsoluteSize.Y)
                    for i,v in pairs(SettingFrameStoreFuncs:GetChildren()) do
                        if v:IsA('Frame') or v:IsA('TextLabel') then
                            totalcanvassize2 = totalcanvassize2+v.AbsoluteSize.Y+5
                        end
                    end
                    MainSettingFrame_2.CanvasSize = UDim2.new(0,0,0,totalcanvassize2)
                    local function move(input)
                        local pos = UDim2.new(math.clamp((input.Position.X - SettingSliderFrame.AbsolutePosition.X) / SettingSliderFrame.AbsoluteSize.X, 0, 1),-6,-2.83333325,0)
                        local pos1 = UDim2.new(math.clamp((input.Position.X - SettingSliderFrame.AbsolutePosition.X) / SettingSliderFrame.AbsoluteSize.X, 0, 1),0,1,0)
                        SettingSliderFrame2:TweenSize(pos1, "Out", "Sine", 0.15, true)
                        SettingSliderCircle:TweenPosition(pos, "Out", "Sine", 0.15, true)
                        currentvalue = math.floor(((pos.X.Scale * (IP2_max or 100)) / (IP2_max or 100)) * ((IP2_max or 100) - (IP2_min or 0)) + (IP2_min or 0))
                        SettingSliderTitle.Text = tostring(IP2_title)..' / '..tostring(GetaFuncs:create_commas(currentvalue))
                        pcall(callback2, currentvalue)
                    end
                    SettingSliderCircle.InputBegan:Connect(function(input)
                        if input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1 then
                            dragging = true
                        end
                    end)
                    SettingSliderCircle.InputEnded:Connect(function(input)
                        if input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1 then
                            dragging = false
                        end
                    end)
                    game:GetService("UserInputService").InputChanged:Connect(function(input)
                        if dragging and input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseMovement then
                            pcall(move,input)
                        end
                    end)
                end
                return ContentSettingFunctions
            end

                local ContentSettingFunctions = {}
                function ContentSettingFunctions:CreateItem(IP2_title)
                    local DropdownItem = Instance.new("Frame")
                    local ItemFrame = Instance.new("Frame")
                    local UICorner = Instance.new("UICorner")
                    local ItemFrame2 = Instance.new("Frame")
                    local UICorner_2 = Instance.new("UICorner")
                    local ItemName = Instance.new("TextButton")

                    if IP_customtheme then
                        ItemFrame.BackgroundTransparency = 1
                        ItemFrame2.BackgroundTransparency = 1
                    end

                    DropdownItem.Name = tostring(IP2_title)
                    DropdownItem.Parent = DropdownContainer
                    DropdownItem.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
                    DropdownItem.BackgroundTransparency = 1.000
                    DropdownItem.Size = UDim2.new(0, 100, 0, 100)

                    ItemFrame.Name = "ItemFrame"
                    ItemFrame.Parent = DropdownItem
                    ItemFrame.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(80, 80, 80)
                    ItemFrame.Size = UDim2.new(0.980000019, 0, 1, 0)

                    UICorner.CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 4)
                    UICorner.Parent = ItemFrame

                    ItemFrame2.Name = "ItemFrame2"
                    ItemFrame2.Parent = ItemFrame
                    ItemFrame2.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(30, 30, 30)
                    ItemFrame2.Position = UDim2.new(0, 2, 0, 2)
                    ItemFrame2.Size = UDim2.new(1, -4, 1, -4)

                    UICorner_2.CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 4)
                    UICorner_2.Parent = ItemFrame2

                    ItemName.Name = "ItemName"
                    ItemName.Parent = ItemFrame2
                    ItemName.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
                    ItemName.BackgroundTransparency = 1.000
                    ItemName.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 1, 0)
                    ItemName.Font = Enum.Font.Gotham
                    ItemName.Text = tostring(IP2_title)
                    ItemName.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
                    ItemName.TextSize = 17.000

                    --DropdownContainerFrame.Size = DropdownContainerFrame.Size+UDim2.new(0,0,0,DropdownItem.AbsoluteSize.Y+5)
                    DropdownContainer.CanvasSize = DropdownContainer.CanvasSize+UDim2.new(0,0,0,DropdownItem.AbsoluteSize.Y+3)
                    ItemName.MouseEnter:Connect(function()
                        GetaFuncs:GetTween(ItemFrame2,0.3,Enum.EasingStyle.Quart,Enum.EasingDirection.Out,{BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(40,40,40)}):Play()
                    end)
                    ItemName.MouseLeave:Connect(function()
                        GetaFuncs:GetTween(ItemFrame2,0.3,Enum.EasingStyle.Quart,Enum.EasingDirection.Out,{BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(30,30,30)}):Play()
                    end)
                    ItemName.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
                        if table.find(dwtablereturn,ItemName.Text) then
                            GetaFuncs:GetTween(ItemName,0.5,Enum.EasingStyle.Quart,Enum.EasingDirection.Out,{TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)}):Play()
                            for i,v in pairs(dwtablereturn) do
                                if v == ItemName.Text then
                                    table.remove(dwtablereturn,i)
                                end
                            end
                        else
                            GetaFuncs:GetTween(ItemName,0.5,Enum.EasingStyle.Quart,Enum.EasingDirection.Out,{TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(0,153,255)}):Play()
                            table.insert(dwtablereturn,ItemName.Text)
                        end
                        if #dwtablereturn == 1 then
                            DropdownValue.Text = dwtablereturn[1]
                        elseif #dwtablereturn > 1 then
                            DropdownValue.Text = ''
                            for i,v in pairs(dwtablereturn) do
                                if i < #dwtablereturn then
                                    DropdownValue.Text = DropdownValue.Text..tostring(v)..', '
                                else                            
                                    DropdownValue.Text = DropdownValue.Text..tostring(v)
                                end
                            end
                        else
                            DropdownValue.Text = ''
                        end
                        pcall(callback,dwtablereturn)
                    end)
                end
                function ContentSettingFunctions:UpdateTitle(IP2_title)
                    DropdownTitle.Text = IP2_title
                end
                function ContentSettingFunctions:UpdateDescription(IP2_desc)
                    DropdownDescription.Text = IP2_desc
                end
                function ContentSettingFunctions:ClearItems()
                    dwtablereturn = {}
                    for i,v in pairs(DropdownContainer:GetChildren()) do
                        if v:IsA('Frame') then
                            v:Destroy()
                        end
                    end
                    DropdownContainer.CanvasSize = UDim2.new(0,0,0,0)
                end
                function ContentSettingFunctions:UpdateItems(IP2_list)
                    dwtablereturn = {}
                    ContentSettingFunctions:ClearItems()
                    wait()
                    for i,v in pairs(IP2_list) do
                        ContentSettingFunctions:CreateItem(tostring(v))
                    end
                end
                function ContentSettingFunctions:AddItem(IP2_name)
                    ContentSettingFunctions:CreateItem(tostring(IP2_name))
                end
                function ContentSettingFunctions:RemoveItem(IP2_name)
                    for i,v in pairs(dwtablereturn) do
                        if v == IP2_name then
                            table.remove(dwtablereturn,i)
                        end
                    end
                    for i,v in pairs(DropdownContainer:GetChildren()) do
                        if v.Name == IP2_name then
                            v:Destroy()
                            DropdownContainer.CanvasSize = DropdownContainer.CanvasSize-UDim2.new(0,0,0,33)
                        end
                    end
                end
                ContentSettingFunctions:UpdateItems(IP_list)

                    local SettingLabel = Instance.new("Frame")

                    wait()
